## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: solid mechanics (materials science) — thermo-mechanical constitutive modeling
**Analysis**: The variables are stress (sigma), strain (epsilon), and temperature (T), which is characteristic of constitutive laws in solid mechanics/materials science describing elastic, plastic, and thermoelastic response with temperature-dependent stiffness and thermal softening.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Hooke’s law (linear elasticity): sigma = c0 * epsilon (small strain, elastic regime)
- Temperature-dependent Hooke’s law: sigma = (c0 + c1 * T) * epsilon (elastic modulus varies approximately linearly with temperature over a limited range)
- Exponential modulus softening: sigma = c0 * exp(c1 * T) * epsilon (rapid stiffness change with temperature)
- Nonlinear elastic (Landau-type expansion): sigma = c0 * epsilon + c1 * epsilon**3 (finite-strain/nonlinear elasticity surrogate)
- Thermoelastic stress with free thermal strain offset: sigma = c0 * (epsilon - c1 * T - c2) (thermal expansion reduces/measures mechanical strain)
- Piecewise elastic–plastic with yield strain: sigma = c0 * epsilon + c1 * Max(epsilon - c2, 0) (bilinear hardening approximation)
- Power-law hardening (Hollomon-type): sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 (plastic flow curve fit over a strain range)
- Temperature-softened power-law hardening: sigma = c0 * epsilon**c1 * exp(c2 * T) (strain hardening with multiplicative thermal softening/stiffening)
- Ramberg–Osgood (implicit, often rearranged): epsilon = c0 * sigma + c1 * sigma**c2 (combined elastic + nonlinear plastic strain; invertible surrogate for sigma(epsilon))
- Hyperbolic tangent transition to plastic flow: sigma = c0 * epsilon + c1 * tanh(c2 * (epsilon - c3)) (smooth elastic-to-plastic transition)
- Johnson–Cook-like thermal softening (strain-only surrogate): sigma = (c0 + c1 * epsilon**c2) * (c3 + c4 * T)**c5 (empirical flow stress with thermal factor; simplified without rate term)
- Eyring/thermal-activation-inspired form: sigma = c0 * asinh(c1 * epsilon) * (c2 + c3 * T) (captures gradual nonlinearity with temperature-dependent scaling)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear elastic region → sigma proportional to epsilon; temperature effects often enter via a temperature-dependent modulus multiplying epsilon.
- Thermal expansion contribution → sigma depends on shifted strain (epsilon - f(T)); stress relaxes toward zero as T increases at fixed total strain if expansion is unconstrained.
- Thermal softening of strength/stiffness → multiplicative factors like exp(c*T) or (c0+c1*T)**c2 reduce sigma with increasing T over relevant ranges.
- Elastic–plastic transition → bilinear or smooth-transition functions (Max(epsilon-c,0), tanh) represent yield onset without introducing extra state variables.
- Strain hardening → sigma scales like epsilon**n (n between 0 and 1 typical for many metals in plastic regime) and may couple with T through multiplicative softening.
- Nonlinear elasticity at moderate strain → odd-power terms (epsilon**3) provide symmetry and capture stiffening/softening beyond Hooke’s law.
- Avoiding negative stresses in tensile-only datasets → use monotone-increasing forms in epsilon (power laws, tanh transitions) unless compression is present.
- Parameter separability often holds approximately → sigma(epsilon,T) ≈ g(epsilon)*h(T) is a common empirical simplification when only epsilon and T are available.
- High-T response sometimes approaches a lower effective modulus/strength → rational or saturating temperature factors (e.g., 1/(c0+c1*T)) can capture asymptotic softening while staying bounded.

**GT:** `90.776*epsilon^2 + 2.482*(T - 337.769)*log(epsilon + 1)`

Expanding: `90.776*epsilon^2 + 2.482*T*log(epsilon+1) - 838.637*log(epsilon+1)`

The GT has three basis functions: `epsilon^2`, `T*log(epsilon+1)`, and `log(epsilon+1)`.

Under the domain constraint (epsilon ≥ 0), `|epsilon| = epsilon` and `Max(0, epsilon) = epsilon`.

Let me systematically check candidates that could potentially match. I'll focus on whether each candidate can produce exactly these three basis functions.

**Candidate 4:**
`(T*c0*epsilon + c1*(T+c2)*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*epsilon*(T+c2) + c5*(T+c2)*|epsilon|^2) / (T+c2)`

= `c0*T*epsilon/(T+c2) + c1*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon^2`

The term `c0*T*epsilon/(T+c2)` is NOT a polynomial in T and epsilon — it's a rational function of T. This cannot match `T*log(epsilon+1)`. Set c0=0 to eliminate it, but then we lose the T-dependence in the log term. **No match.**

Wait, let me re-examine. The GT needs `T*log(epsilon+1)`. Candidate 4's only T-dependent term besides the rational one is... let me re-expand:

`= T*c0*epsilon/(T+c2) + c1*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon^2`

This has no `T*log(epsilon+1)` term. **No match.**

**Candidate 10:**
`(c0*epsilon + (c1*epsilon+c2)*(T*c3*epsilon + c4*|epsilon| + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1))) / (c1*epsilon+c2)`

= `c0*epsilon/(c1*epsilon+c2) + T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1)`

With epsilon≥0: `= c0*epsilon/(c1*epsilon+c2) + T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1)`

GT needs `T*log(epsilon+1)` but this has `T*c3*epsilon`. These are different basis functions. Unless c3=0, but then no T-dependence. **No match.**

**Candidate 11:**
`(c0*epsilon + (T*c1+c2)*(T*c3*epsilon + c4*|epsilon| + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1))) / (T*c1+c2)`

= `c0*epsilon/(T*c1+c2) + T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1)`

The first term is rational in T. Set c0=0: `T*c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*epsilon+1)`. No `epsilon^2` or `T*log` term. **No match.**

**Candidate 12:**
`T*c0*epsilon + c1*|epsilon| + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

With epsilon≥0: `T*c0*epsilon + (c1+c0*T... wait: = (c0*T + c1)*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

Basis functions: `T*epsilon`, `epsilon`, `log(c3*epsilon+1)`, `log(c5*epsilon+1)`. GT needs `epsilon^2` and `T*log(epsilon+1)`. No `epsilon^2` term and no `T*log` coupling. **No match.**

**Candidate 19:**
`(T*(T*c0+c1)*|epsilon| + c2*(T+c3)*log(c4*epsilon+1) + c5*epsilon) / (T+c3)`

With epsilon≥0:
= `T*(T*c0+c1)*epsilon/(T+c3) + c2*log(c4*epsilon+1) + c5*epsilon/(T+c3)`

= `(T^2*c0 + T*c1)*epsilon/(T+c3) + c2*log(c4*epsilon+1) + c5*epsilon/(T+c3)`

If c0=0: `(T*c1*epsilon + c5*epsilon)/(T+c3) + c2*log(c4*epsilon+1)` = `(c1*T+c5)*epsilon/(T+c3) + c2*log(c4*epsilon+1)`

If c1=c5/c3... this is still rational in T, not polynomial. We need `epsilon^2` and `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **No match.**

Let me look for candidates with both `epsilon^2` (or `|epsilon|^2`) AND `T*log(epsilon+1)` terms.

**Candidate 2:**
`c0*|epsilon|^2 + c1*epsilon + c2*log(T*c3+1)*|epsilon| + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

= `c0*epsilon^2 + c1*epsilon + c2*log(c3*T+1)*epsilon + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

Basis: `epsilon^2`, `epsilon`, `log(c3*T+1)*epsilon`, `log(c5*epsilon+1)`.

GT needs `T*log(epsilon+1)`. This has `log(c3*T+1)*epsilon` instead. `log(c3*T+1)` ≠ `T` for any constant. **No match.**

**Candidate 14:**
`T*c0*log(c1*|epsilon|+1) + c2*|epsilon|^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(c1*|epsilon|+1) + c5*log(T*c6+1)*|epsilon|`

= `c2*epsilon^2 + c3*epsilon + (c0*T+c4)*log(c1*epsilon+1) + c5*log(c6*T+1)*epsilon`

Basis: `epsilon^2`, `epsilon`, `T*log(c1*epsilon+1)`, `log(c1*epsilon+1)`, `log(c6*T+1)*epsilon`.

Set c5=0, c1=1: `c2*epsilon^2 + c3*epsilon + (c0*T+c4)*log(epsilon+1)`

= `c2*epsilon^2 + c3*epsilon + c0*T*log(epsilon+1) + c4*log(epsilon+1)`

GT = `90.776*epsilon^2 + 2.482*T*log(epsilon+1) - 838.637*log(epsilon+1)`

Set c2=90.776, c3=0, c0=2.482, c4=-838.637. **This matches!**

**Candidate 14 verdict: [MATCH]**

Let me continue checking other promising candidates.

**Candidate 30:**
`T*c0*epsilon + c1*|epsilon| + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*log(T*c5+1)*|epsilon|^2`

= `(c0*T+c1)*epsilon + c2*log(c3*epsilon+1) + c4*log(c5*T+1)*epsilon^2`

Has `log(T*c5+1)*epsilon^2` instead of `epsilon^2`. **No match.**

**Candidate 40:**
`c0*|epsilon| + c1*log(c2*epsilon+1) + c3*log(T*c4+1)*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

= `c0*epsilon + c1*log(c2*epsilon+1) + c3*log(c4*T+1)*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

No `epsilon^2`. **No match.**

**Candidate 44:**
`(c0*epsilon + (c1*epsilon+c2)*(c3*|epsilon|^2 + c4*epsilon + c5*log(T*c6+1)*|epsilon|)) / (c1*epsilon+c2)`

= `c0*epsilon/(c1*epsilon+c2) + c3*epsilon^2 + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*T+1)*epsilon`

Set c0=0: `c3*epsilon^2 + c4*epsilon + c5*log(c6*T+1)*epsilon`. Has `log(T)` not `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **No match.**

**Candidate 46:**
Same structure as 44 but with `(T*c1+c2)`. Similar issue. **No match.**

**Candidate 47:**
`(T*c0*epsilon + (T+c1)*(c2*|epsilon|^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(T*c5+1)*|epsilon|)) / (T+c1)`

= `T*c0*epsilon/(T+c1) + c2*epsilon^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(c5*T+1)*epsilon`

Set c0=0: `c2*epsilon^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(c5*T+1)*epsilon`. No `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **No match.**

**Candidate 62:**
`T*c0*epsilon + c1*|epsilon| + c2*epsilon*log(T*c3+1) + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

= `(c0*T+c1)*epsilon + c2*epsilon*log(c3*T+1) + c4*log(c5*epsilon+1)`

Basis: `T*epsilon`, `epsilon`, `epsilon*log(c3*T+1)`, `log(c5*epsilon+1)`. GT needs `epsilon^2` and `T*log(epsilon+1)`. No `epsilon^2`. **No match.**

**Candidate 61:**
`(c0*|epsilon|^2 + (c1+|epsilon|^2)*(c2*|epsilon|^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(T*c5+1)*|epsilon|)) / (c1+|epsilon|^2)`

= `c0*epsilon^2/(c1+epsilon^2) + c2*epsilon^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(c5*T+1)*epsilon`

Rational term + no `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **No match.**

Now let me verify Candidate 14 more carefully:

GT: `90.776*epsilon^2 + 2.482*(T-337.769)*log(epsilon+1)` = `90.776*epsilon^2 + 2.482*T*log(epsilon+1) - 838.637*log(epsilon+1)`

Candidate 14: `T*c0*log(c1*|epsilon|+1) + c2*|epsilon|^2 + c3*epsilon + c4*log(c1*|epsilon|+1) + c5*log(T*c6+1)*|epsilon|`

With epsilon≥0 and setting c5=0, c1=1, c3=0:
= `c0*T*log(epsilon+1) + c2*epsilon^2 + c4*log(epsilon+1)`

This exactly matches GT with c0=2.482, c2=90.776, c4=-838.637. ✓

Now let me quickly scan remaining candidates for any with `T*log(epsilon+1)` + `epsilon^2`:

**Candidate 6:**
Simplifies to: `c0*epsilon/(c2*epsilon+c3) + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon^2`
No log terms with T. **No match.**

**Candidate 36:**
`(T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon*(T+c2)*exp(T*c3) + c4*epsilon*(T+c2) + c5*(T+c2)*|epsilon|^2) / (T+c2)`
= `T*c0*epsilon/(T+c2) + c1*epsilon*exp(T*c3) + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon^2`
Exponential in T, no log. **No match.**

**Candidate 35:**
= `T*c0*epsilon/(T+c2) + c1*sin(c3*epsilon) + c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon^2`
Has sin, no T*log. **No match.**

**Candidate 84:**
`(T*(T*c0+c1)*|epsilon| + c2*(T+c3)*log(T*c4+1)*log(c5*|epsilon|+1) + c6*epsilon) / (T+c3)`

= `T*(T*c0+c1)*epsilon/(T+c3) + c2*log(c4*T+1)*log(c5*epsilon+1) + c6*epsilon/(T+c3)`

Has `log(T)*log(epsilon)` not `T*log(epsilon)`. **No match.**

Let me also check candidates with fraction structures more carefully:

**Candidate 90:**
`(T*c0+c1 + (c2*epsilon+c3)*(T*c4*epsilon + c5*|epsilon| + c6*epsilon*log(T*c7+1))) / (c2*epsilon+c3)`

= `(T*c0+c1)/(c2*epsilon+c3) + T*c4*epsilon + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon*log(c7*T+1)`

No `epsilon^2` or `T*log(epsilon+1)`. **No match.**
